\doxysubsection{Detailed Description}
Contains {\itshape low-\/level} functions and variables of the \textbackslash{}\+CImg Library. 

Most of the functions and variables within this namespace are used by the \textbackslash{}\+CImg library for low-\/level operations. You may use them to access specific const values or environment variables internally used by \textbackslash{}\+CImg. \begin{DoxyWarning}{Warning}
Never write {\ttfamily using namespace \doxylink{namespacecimg__library_1_1cimg}{cimg\+\_\+library\+::cimg};} in your source code. Lot of functions in the {\ttfamily cimg\+:\+: namespace} have the same names as standard C functions that may be defined in the global namespace {\ttfamily \+::}. 
\end{DoxyWarning}

\Hypertarget{namespacecimg__library_1_1cimg_a76a19188a831d32455decb865e33d289}\index{cimg\_library::cimg@{cimg\_library::cimg}!curl\_path@{curl\_path}}

\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{curl\_path()}{curl\_path()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \label{namespacecimg__library_1_1cimg_a76a19188a831d32455decb865e33d289} 
const char \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*} cimg\+\_\+library\+::cimg\+::curl\+\_\+path (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{const char \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}const}]{user\+\_\+path}{, }\item[{const bool}]{reinit\+\_\+path}{}\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [inline]}}



Search path of an executable. 

Get the file or directory attributes with support for UTF-\/8 paths (Windows only). Get/set path to the {\itshape Program Files/} directory (Windows only). 
\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em user\+\_\+path} & Specified path, or {\ttfamily 0} to get the path currently used. \\
\hline
{\em reinit\+\_\+path} & Force path to be recalculated (may take some time). \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}

{\footnotesize\ttfamily \label{namespacecimg__library_1_1cimg_aa11c5d563db3cf0a03e6ce6335aac835} 
template$<$typename t$>$ \\
int cimg\+\_\+library\+::cimg\+::dialog (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{const char \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}const}]{title}{, }\item[{const char \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}const}]{msg}{, }\item[{const char \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}const}]{button1\+\_\+label}{, }\item[{const char \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}const}]{button2\+\_\+label}{, }\item[{const char \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}const}]{button3\+\_\+label}{, }\item[{const char \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}const}]{button4\+\_\+label}{, }\item[{const char \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}const}]{button5\+\_\+label}{, }\item[{const char \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}const}]{button6\+\_\+label}{, }\item[{const \mbox{\hyperlink{structcimg__library_1_1CImg}{CImg}}$<$ t $>$ \&}]{logo}{, }\item[{const bool}]{is\+\_\+centered}{ = {\ttfamily false}}\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [inline]}}



Display a simple dialog box, and wait for the user\textquotesingle{}s response. 


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em title} & Title of the dialog window. \\
\hline
{\em msg} & Main message displayed inside the dialog window. \\
\hline
{\em button1\+\_\+label} & Label of the 1st button. \\
\hline
{\em button2\+\_\+label} & Label of the 2nd button ({\ttfamily 0} to hide button). \\
\hline
{\em button3\+\_\+label} & Label of the 3rd button ({\ttfamily 0} to hide button). \\
\hline
{\em button4\+\_\+label} & Label of the 4th button ({\ttfamily 0} to hide button). \\
\hline
{\em button5\+\_\+label} & Label of the 5th button ({\ttfamily 0} to hide button). \\
\hline
{\em button6\+\_\+label} & Label of the 6th button ({\ttfamily 0} to hide button). \\
\hline
{\em logo} & Image logo displayed at the left of the main message. \\
\hline
{\em is\+\_\+centered} & Tells if the dialog window must be centered on the screen. \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
Index of clicked button (from {\ttfamily 0} to {\ttfamily 5}), or {\ttfamily -\/1} if the dialog window has been closed by the user. 
\end{DoxyReturn}
\begin{DoxyNote}{Note}

\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item Up to 6 buttons can be defined in the dialog window.
\item The function returns when a user clicked one of the button or closed the dialog window.
\item If a button text is set to 0, the corresponding button (and the following) will not appear in the dialog box. At least one button must be specified. 
\end{DoxyItemize}
\end{DoxyNote}

\Hypertarget{namespacecimg__library_1_1cimg_aa11ed1e7e4489216ea90a3bc150638df}\index{cimg\_library::cimg@{cimg\_library::cimg}!exception\_mode@{exception\_mode}}
\index{exception\_mode@{exception\_mode}!cimg\_library::cimg@{cimg\_library::cimg}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{exception\_mode()}{exception\_mode()}\hspace{0.1cm}{\footnotesize\ttfamily [2/3]}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \label{namespacecimg__library_1_1cimg_aa11ed1e7e4489216ea90a3bc150638df} 
unsigned int \& cimg\+\_\+library\+::cimg\+::exception\+\_\+mode (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{const unsigned int}]{mode}{}\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [inline]}}



Set current \textbackslash{}\+CImg exception mode. 

The way error messages are handled by \textbackslash{}\+CImg can be changed dynamically, using this function. 
\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em mode} & Desired exception mode. Possible values are\+:
\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item {\ttfamily 0}\+: Hide library messages (quiet mode).
\item {\ttfamily 1}\+: Print library messages on the console.
\item {\ttfamily 2}\+: Display library messages on a dialog window.
\item {\ttfamily 3}\+: Do as {\ttfamily 1} + add extra debug warnings (slow down the code!).
\item {\ttfamily 4}\+: Do as {\ttfamily 2} + add extra debug warnings (slow down the code!). 
\end{DoxyItemize}\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\Hypertarget{namespacecimg__library_1_1cimg_af9e84f4cf15bbc0dc56a0d70a391a95d}\index{cimg\_library::cimg@{cimg\_library::cimg}!exception\_mode@{exception\_mode}}

char \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*} cimg\+\_\+library\+::cimg\+::load\+\_\+network (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{const char \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}const}]{url}{, }\item[{char \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}const}]{filename\+\_\+local}{, }\item[{const unsigned int}]{timeout}{, }\item[{const bool}]{try\+\_\+fallback}{, }\item[{const char \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}const}]{referer}{, }\item[{const char \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}const}]{user\+\_\+agent}{}\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [inline]}}



Load file from network as a local temporary file. 


\begin{DoxyParams}[1]{Parameters}
 & {\em url} & URL of the filename, as a C-\/string. \\
\hline
\mbox{\texttt{ out}}  & {\em filename\+\_\+local} & C-\/string containing the path to a local copy of {\ttfamily filename}. \\
\hline
 & {\em timeout} & Maximum time (in seconds) authorized for downloading the file from the URL. \\
\hline
 & {\em try\+\_\+fallback} & When using libcurl, tells using system calls as fallbacks in case of libcurl failure. \\
\hline
 & {\em referer} & Referer used, as a C-\/string. \\
\hline
 & {\em user\+\_\+agent} & User agent used, as a C-\/string. \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
Value of {\ttfamily filename\+\_\+local}. 
\end{DoxyReturn}
\begin{DoxyNote}{Note}
Use the {\ttfamily libcurl} library, or the external binaries {\ttfamily wget} or {\ttfamily curl} to perform the download. 
\end{DoxyNote}

{\footnotesize\ttfamily \label{namespacecimg__library_1_1cimg_a5515802906984683da51c081da768759} 
template$<$typename T$>$ \\
T cimg\+\_\+library\+::cimg\+::minmod (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{const T \&}]{a}{, }\item[{const T \&}]{b}{}\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [inline]}}



Return the min-\/mod of two values. 

\begin{DoxyNote}{Note}
{\itshape minmod({\ttfamily a},{\ttfamily b})} is defined to be\+:
\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item {\itshape minmod({\ttfamily a},{\ttfamily b}) = min({\ttfamily a},{\ttfamily b})}, if {\ttfamily a} and {\ttfamily b} have the same sign.
\item {\itshape minmod({\ttfamily a},{\ttfamily b}) = 0}, if {\ttfamily a} and {\ttfamily b} have different signs. 
\end{DoxyItemize}
\end{DoxyNote}

Return current \textbackslash{}\+CImg openmp mode. 

\Hypertarget{namespacecimg__library_1_1cimg_a301fafb1df82e19f97d9ec184ed6c1ad}\index{cimg\_library::cimg@{cimg\_library::cimg}!openmp\_mode@{openmp\_mode}}
\index{openmp\_mode@{openmp\_mode}!cimg\_library::cimg@{cimg\_library::cimg}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{openmp\_mode()}{openmp\_mode()}\hspace{0.1cm}{\footnotesize\ttfamily [2/3]}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \label{namespacecimg__library_1_1cimg_a301fafb1df82e19f97d9ec184ed6c1ad} 
unsigned int cimg\+\_\+library\+::cimg\+::openmp\+\_\+mode (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{const unsigned int}]{mode}{}\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [inline]}}



Set current \textbackslash{}\+CImg openmp mode. 

The way openmp-\/based methods are handled by \textbackslash{}\+CImg can be changed dynamically, using this function. 
\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em mode} & Desired openmp mode. Possible values are\+:
\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item {\ttfamily 0}\+: Never parallelize.
\item {\ttfamily 1}\+: Always parallelize.
\item {\ttfamily 2}\+: Adaptive parallelization mode (default behavior). 
\end{DoxyItemize}\\

\end{DoxyReturn}

\Hypertarget{namespacecimg__library_1_1cimg_a3c8917c0f12139bff6de6e3e45fc5b77}\index{cimg\_library::cimg@{cimg\_library::cimg}!wait@{wait}}
\index{wait@{wait}!cimg\_library::cimg@{cimg\_library::cimg}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{wait()}{wait()}\hspace{0.1cm}{\footnotesize\ttfamily [1/2]}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \label{namespacecimg__library_1_1cimg_a3c8917c0f12139bff6de6e3e45fc5b77} 
unsigned int cimg\+\_\+library\+::cimg\+::wait (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{const unsigned int}]{milliseconds}{}\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [inline]}}



Wait for a given number of milliseconds since the last call to \doxylink{namespacecimg__library_1_1cimg_aaff5f4b4193e67534ba4f6adc3ddbc66}{wait()}. 


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em milliseconds} & Number of milliseconds to wait for. \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
Number of milliseconds elapsed since the last call to \doxylink{namespacecimg__library_1_1cimg_aaff5f4b4193e67534ba4f6adc3ddbc66}{wait()}. 
\end{DoxyReturn}
\begin{DoxyNote}{Note}
Same as \doxylink{namespacecimg__library_1_1cimg_a3ac7655e49556a90715f3532af221334}{sleep()} with a waiting time computed with regard to the last call of \doxylink{namespacecimg__library_1_1cimg_aaff5f4b4193e67534ba4f6adc3ddbc66}{wait()}. It may be used to temporize your program properly, without wasting CPU time. 
\end{DoxyNote}

\Hypertarget{namespacecimg__library_1_1cimg_a5ee7f021ed42b0ac32e1254414c3faab}\index{cimg\_library::cimg@{cimg\_library::cimg}!warn@{warn}}
\index{warn@{warn}!cimg\_library::cimg@{cimg\_library::cimg}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{warn()}{warn()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \label{namespacecimg__library_1_1cimg_a5ee7f021ed42b0ac32e1254414c3faab} 
void cimg\+\_\+library\+::cimg\+::warn (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{const char \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}const}]{format}{, }\item[{}]{...}{}\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [inline]}}



Display a warning message on the default output stream. 


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em format} & C-\/string containing the format of the message, as with {\ttfamily std\+::printf()}. \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyNote}{Note}
If configuration macro {\ttfamily cimg\+\_\+strict\+\_\+warnings} is set, this function throws a {\ttfamily \doxylink{structcimg__library_1_1CImgWarningException}{CImg\+Warning\+Exception}} instead. 
\end{DoxyNote}
\begin{DoxyWarning}{Warning}
As the first argument is a format string, it is highly recommended to write 
\begin{DoxyCode}{0}
\DoxyCodeLine{\mbox{\hyperlink{namespacecimg__library_1_1cimg_a5ee7f021ed42b0ac32e1254414c3faab}{cimg::warn}}(\textcolor{stringliteral}{"{}\%s"{}},warning\_message);}

\end{DoxyCode}
 instead of 
\begin{DoxyCode}{0}
\DoxyCodeLine{\mbox{\hyperlink{namespacecimg__library_1_1cimg_a5ee7f021ed42b0ac32e1254414c3faab}{cimg::warn}}(warning\_message);}

\end{DoxyCode}
 if {\ttfamily warning\+\_\+message} can be arbitrary, to prevent nasty memory access. 
\end{DoxyWarning}
